Notice	
	
..	
47
Notice
No Legal responsibility is accepted for the publication of advertisements regarding 
change of name in the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette. Persons notifying the changes 
will remain solely responsible for the legal consequences and also for any other 
misrepresentation, etc.
(By  Order)
Director  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

Public NoticES
Raja Pandi. V, a male Child born to Thiru Velusamy on 7th April 1991 residing at No. 7/12, J.J. Nagar, Sakthivinayaga 
Aravani Colony, Neripperichal, Tiruppur-641 602. Living as transgender after an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery 
examined by medical Board, Government Head Quarters Hospital, Tiruppur District. By this I, may be treated as a transgender 
and shall henceforth be known as Kavi. V.
Tiruppur, 	
	
V. Rajapandi.
27th December 2018.
Loganathan. N, a male Child born to Thiru Nagarajan on 24th April 1980 residing at No. 44/1, Cell Tower, Arukil 
G.N. Nagar, Thottathupalayam, Neripperichal, Tiruppur, Puluvapatti-641 602. Living as transgender after an elaborate sexual 
reassignment 
surgery 
examined 
by 
medical 
Board, 
Government 
Head 
Quarters 
Hospital, 
Tiruppur 
District. 
By  this  I, may be treated as a transgender and shall henceforth be known as Avanthika. N.
Tiruppur, 	
	 	
N. Loganathan
27th December 2018.
